INPUT: === architecture.md ===
# Content Publishing Hub Architecture

## Overview
The system is a web-based Content Publishing Hub that manages articles with version control, approvals, analytics, and scheduling. It comprises frontend and backend components developed using Flask.

## Backend Responsibilities
- Manage data storage for articles, versions, approvals, analytics, users, and workflow stages.
- Provide RESTful API endpoints for article CRUD operations, version management, approval workflow, analytics data retrieval, and scheduling.
- Handle authentication and authorization.
- Implement control flow for publishing stages: draft, review, approval, published, rejected.
- Save and retrieve article versions, manage approval status, and track analytics metrics such as views, unique visitors, and average read time.

## Frontend Responsibilities
- Render pages for article creation, editing, version comparison, analytics dashboard, calendar view, and approval workflows.
- Support form inputs for new articles, editing content, filtering and sorting articles by status, category, and stage.
- Display analytics visualizations such as total views and unique visitors per article.
- Provide controls and workflows for approvals, version restoration, and scheduling publishing.

## API Design and Routing
- `GET /articles`: List articles with filtering by status (`filter_status`), category (`filter_category`), and author.
- `POST /article/create`: Create a new article.
- `GET /article/<article_id>`: Retrieve a specific article's metadata and current version.
- `POST /article/<article_id>/edit`: Edit an article's content.
- `GET /article/<article_id>/versions`: Retrieve all versions of an article.
- `POST /article/<article_id>/version/<version_id>/restore`: Restore a previous version.
- `GET /article/<article_id>/analytics`: Retrieve analytics data (views, unique visitors).
- `POST /article/<article_id>/approve`: Submit article for approval or change approval status.
- `GET /dashboard`: Retrieve user's dashboard data.
- `GET /calendar`: Retrieve publishing schedule events.

## Frontend Templates and Components
- `dashboard.html`: User dashboard overview.
- `create_article.html`: Form to create a new article.
- `edit_article.html`: Editing page with title and content fields.
- `version_history.html`: List and compare article versions.
- `article_analytics.html`: Show article performance statistics.
- `content_calendar.html`: Calendar view of scheduled articles.
- `published_articles.html`: List of published articles with filters.
- `my_articles.html`: User's articles.

## Data Flow and Integration
- Frontend sends requests with filters, article IDs, and version IDs.
- Backend responds with JSON for API calls or rendered HTML templates.
- Versioning controlled by storing metadata such as version_number, stage (draft, review, approved)
- Approval status controls rendering and workflow progression.
- Analytics data updated incrementally on article views.

## Workflow Control
- Articles move through stages: draft -> under_review -> approved/rejected -> published.
- Interaction with approval buttons and filters for visualization.
- Scheduling managed via calendar interface with status indicators.

## Authentication and User Management
- User credentials stored in `users.txt` with email and fullname.
- Permissions defined by role (Admin, Editor, Publisher).
- Secure route access using session or token-based authentication.

## Technologies
- Flask for backend
- Jinja2 for templating
- JavaScript for frontend interactions
- Data stored in flat files (e.g., `articles.txt`, `article_versions.txt`, `approvals.txt`, `analytics.txt`)

# Conclusion
This architecture ensures modular separation between frontend rendering and backend data management, supports rich versioning and approval workflows, and provides detailed analytics and scheduling features suitable for a content publishing platform.

Functional Test Feedback for Content Publishing Hub

Note: The backend source code (app.py) is not available. Therefore, full dynamic functional testing, including backend data interaction and route execution, cannot be performed. This feedback is based on static analysis of templates and inferred functionalities.

1. Dashboard (/dashboard)
- All required elements with correct IDs are present (dashboard-page, btn-create-article, btn-my-articles, btn-published-articles, btn-content-calendar, dashboard-overview).
- Navigation links to create article, my articles, published articles, and content calendar are correctly identified.

2. Create Article (/create_article)
- The form has the correct elements with IDs, including article-title, article-content, btn-submit-article.
- Form method POST and action URL placeholder correct.
- Back to Dashboard button present with expected ID.

3. My Articles (/my_articles)
- Filter form with status and category dropdowns has correct IDs.
- The articles table (my-articles-table) has required columns.
- Each article's action includes version history and analytics links with proper IDs referencing article IDs.
- Navigation links to dashboard and create article present.

4. Published Articles (/published_articles)
- Filter form is present with correct controls for filtering by status and category.
- Published articles table contains required columns and uses correct IDs.
- Back to dashboard navigation link present.

5. Content Calendar (/content_calendar)
- Page container and elements have correct IDs.
- Navigation link back to dashboard confirmed.
- Placeholder text for calendar UI present.

6. Edit Article (/edit_article)
- Edit article form with IDs: edit-article-form, article-title, article-content, btn-save-changes.
- Prefilled values shown by {{ article.title }} and {{ article.content }} placeholders.
- Back to Dashboard button present.

7. Version History (/version_history)
- Versions table with columns: Version Number, Date, Stage, Actions.
- Restore version button with unique IDs per version.
- Navigation back to article editing present.

8. Article Analytics (/article_analytics)
- Analytics data section present with performance metric elements: views-count, unique-visitors-count, average-read-time.
- Back to article editing button present.

Defects and Issues:
- Cannot verify dynamic backend functionality, route handling, form submission processing, version restoration, or analytics data feeding due to missing app.py.
- No obvious issues found in static templates, element IDs are consistent and appropriate.
- Some links use button onclick with window.location.href; could be improved to use anchor tags for accessibility.
- No ARIA roles or accessibility features found in templates, consider adding for better accessibility.
- Templates reference dynamic data placeholders; need backend integration to verify data accuracy and rendering.

Suggestions:
- Provide backend source code to enable complete functional testing of routing, data processing, and database interactions.
- Implement automated functional tests covering form submissions, filtering, versioning, and analytical report generation.
- Enhance UI accessibility and consider client-side validation for forms.

Status: NEED_MODIFY

Published Articles (/published_articles) - Filter form is present with correct controls for filtering by status and category. - Published articles table contains required columns and uses correct IDs. - Back to dashboard navigation link present.  5. Content Calendar (/content_calendar) - Page container and elements have correct IDs. - Navigation link back to dashboard confirmed. - Placeholder text for calendar UI present.  6. Edit Article (/edit_article) - Edit article form with IDs: edit-article-form, article-title, article-content, btn-save-changes. - Prefilled values shown by {{ article.title }} and {{ article.content }} placeholders. - Back to Dashboard button present.  7. Version History (/version_history) - Versions table with columns: Version Number, Date, Stage, Actions. - Restore version button with unique IDs per version. - Navigation back to article editing present.  8. Article Analytics (/article_analytics) - Analytics data section present with performance metric elements: views-count, unique-visitors-count, average-read-time. - Back to article editing button present.  Defects and Issues: - Cannot verify dynamic backend functionality, route handling, form submission processing, version restoration, or analytics data feeding due to missing app.py. - No obvious issues found in static templates, element IDs are consistent and appropriate. - Some links use button onclick with window.location.href; could be improved to use anchor tags for accessibility. - No ARIA roles or accessibility features found in templates, consider adding for better accessibility. - Templates reference dynamic data placeholders; need backend integration to verify data accuracy and rendering.  Suggestions: - Provide backend source code to enable complete functional testing of routing, data processing, and database interactions. - Implement automated functional tests covering form submissions, filtering, versioning, and analytical report generation. - Enhance UI accessibility and consider client-side validation for forms.  Status: NEED_MODIFY

My Articles (/my_articles) - Filter form with status and category dropdowns has correct IDs. - The articles table (my-articles-table) has required columns. - Each article's action includes version history and analytics links with proper IDs referencing article IDs. - Navigation links to dashboard and create article present.  4. Published Articles (/published_articles) - Filter form is present with correct controls for filtering by status and category. - Published articles table contains required columns and uses correct IDs. - Back to dashboard navigation link present.  5. Content Calendar (/content_calendar) - Page container and elements have correct IDs. - Navigation link back to dashboard confirmed. - Placeholder text for calendar UI present.  6. Edit Article (/edit_article) - Edit article form with IDs: edit-article-form, article-title, article-content, btn-save-changes. - Prefilled values shown by {{ article.title }} and {{ article.content }} placeholders. - Back to Dashboard button present.  7. Version History (/version_history) - Versions table with columns: Version Number, Date, Stage, Actions. - Restore version button with unique IDs per version. - Navigation back to article editing present.  8. Article Analytics (/article_analytics) - Analytics data section present with performance metric elements: views-count, unique-visitors-count, average-read-time. - Back to article editing button present.  Defects and Issues: - Cannot verify dynamic backend functionality, route handling, form submission processing, version restoration, or analytics data feeding due to missing app.py. - No obvious issues found in static templates, element IDs are consistent and appropriate. - Some links use button onclick with window.location.href; could be improved to use anchor tags for accessibility. - No ARIA roles or accessibility features found in templates, consider adding for better accessibility. - Templates reference dynamic data placeholders; need backend integration to verify data accuracy and rendering.  Suggestions: - Provide backend source code to enable complete functional testing of routing, data processing, and database interactions. - Implement automated functional tests covering form submissions, filtering, versioning, and analytical report generation. - Enhance UI accessibility and consider client-side validation for forms. Functional Test Feedback for Content Publishing Hub

Note: The backend source code (app.py) is not available. Therefore, full dynamic functional testing, including backend data interaction and route execution, cannot be performed. This feedback is based on static analysis of templates and inferred functionalities.

1. Dashboard (/dashboard)
- All required elements with correct IDs are present (dashboard-page, btn-create-article, btn-my-articles, btn-published-articles, btn-content-calendar, dashboard-overview).
- Navigation links to create article, my articles, published articles, and content calendar are correctly identified.

2. Create Article (/create_article)
- The form has the correct elements with IDs, including article-title, article-content, btn-submit-article.
- Form method POST and action URL placeholder correct.
- Back to Dashboard button present with expected ID.

3. My Articles (/my_articles)
- Filter form with status and category dropdowns has correct IDs.
- The articles table (my-articles-table) has required columns.
- Each article's action includes version history and analytics links with proper IDs referencing article IDs.
- Navigation links to dashboard and create article present.

4. Published Articles (/published_articles)
- Filter form is present with correct controls for filtering by status and category.
- Published articles table contains required columns and uses correct IDs.
- Back to dashboard navigation link present.

5. Content Calendar (/content_calendar)
- Page container and elements have correct IDs.
- Navigation link back to dashboard confirmed.
- Placeholder text for calendar UI present.

6. Edit Article (/edit_article)
- Edit article form with IDs: edit-article-form, article-title, article-content, btn-save-changes.
- Prefilled values shown by {{ article.title }} and {{ article.content }} placeholders.
- Back to Dashboard button present.

7. Version History (/version_history)
- Versions table with columns: Version Number, Date, Stage, Actions.
- Restore version button with unique IDs per version.
- Navigation back to article editing present.

8. Article Analytics (/article_analytics)
- Analytics data section present with performance metric elements: views-count, unique-visitors-count, average-read-time.
- Back to article editing button present.

Defects and Issues:
- Cannot verify dynamic backend functionality, route handling, form submission processing, version restoration, or analytics data feeding due to missing app.py.
- No obvious issues found in static templates, element IDs are consistent and appropriate.
- Some links use button onclick with window.location.href; could be improved to use anchor tags for accessibility.
- No ARIA roles or accessibility features found in templates, consider adding for better accessibility.
- Templates reference dynamic data placeholders; need backend integration to verify data accuracy and rendering.

Suggestions:
- Provide backend source code to enable complete functional testing of routing, data processing, and database interactions.
- Implement automated functional tests covering form submissions, filtering, versioning, and analytical report generation.
- Enhance UI accessibility and consider client-side validation for forms.

from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)

# Mock data stores
articles = {}
article_versions = {}
article_analytics_data = {}

# A simple auto-increment ID generator for articles and versions
next_article_id = 1

# Article statuses
STATUSES = ['draft', 'under_review', 'approved', 'rejected', 'published', 'archived']

# Categories example
CATEGORIES = ['Technology', 'Science', 'Lifestyle', 'Health', 'Finance']


@app.route('/')
def root():
    # Redirect to dashboard
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))


@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    return render_template('dashboard.html')


@app.route('/create_article', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def create_article():
    global next_article_id
    if request.method == 'POST':
        title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
        content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()
        if not title or not content:
            abort(400, 'Title and content are required')
        article_id = next_article_id
        next_article_id += 1
        articles[article_id] = {
            'id': article_id,
            'title': title,
            'content': content,
            'status': 'draft',
            'category': 'Uncategorized',
            'last_modified': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
            'author': 'Current User',  # Placeholder
            'published_date': None
        }
        # Initialize versions list
        article_versions[article_id] = [
            {
                'id': 1,
                'version_number': 1,
                'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
                'stage': 'draft',
                'title': title,
                'content': content
            }
        ]
        # Initialize analytics
        article_analytics_data[article_id] = {
            'views': 0,
            'unique_visitors': 0,
            'average_read_time': 0
        }
        return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))
    else:
        return render_template('create_article.html')


@app.route('/my_articles')
def my_articles():
    filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'all')
    filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')

    filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values()]
    if filter_status != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]
    if filter_category != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]

    return render_template('my_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)


@app.route('/published_articles')
def published_articles():
    filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'published')
    filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')

    filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values() if a['status'] in ['published', 'archived']]
    if filter_status != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]
    if filter_category != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]

    return render_template('published_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)


@app.route('/content_calendar')
def content_calendar():
    # For simplicity, we just render the page without dynamic data
    return render_template('content_calendar.html')


@app.route('/edit_article/<int:article_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def edit_article(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')

    if request.method == 'POST':
        title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
        content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()
        if not title or not content:
            abort(400, 'Title and content are required')
        article['title'] = title
        article['content'] = content
        article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

        # Save a new version
        versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
        version_number = len(versions) + 1
        new_version = {
            'id': version_number,
            'version_number': version_number,
            'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
            'stage': article['status'],
            'title': title,
            'content': content
        }
        versions.append(new_version)
        article_versions[article_id] = versions

        return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))
    else:
        return render_template('edit_article.html', article=article)


@app.route('/version_history/<int:article_id>')
def version_history(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')
    versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
    return render_template('version_history.html', article=article, versions=versions)


@app.route('/restore_version/<int:article_id>/<int:version_id>', methods=['POST'])
def restore_version(article_id, version_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')

    versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
    version_to_restore = None
    for v in versions:
        if v['id'] == version_id:
            version_to_restore = v
            break

    if not version_to_restore:
        abort(404, 'Version not found')

    # Restore content from version
    article['title'] = version_to_restore['title']
    article['content'] = version_to_restore['content']
    article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

    # Save a new version as this restore event
    version_number = len(versions) + 1
    new_version = {
        'id': version_number,
        'version_number': version_number,
        'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
        'stage': article['status'],
        'title': article['title'],
        'content': article['content']
    }
    versions.append(new_version)
    article_versions[article_id] = versions

    return redirect(url_for('edit_article', article_id=article_id))


@app.route('/article_analytics/<int:article_id>')
def article_analytics(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')
    analytics = article_analytics_data.get(article_id, {
        'views': 0,
        'unique_visitors': 0,
        'average_read_time': 0
    })
    return render_template('article_analytics.html', article=article, analytics=analytics)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)

- Published articles table contains required columns and uses correct IDs.
- Back to dashboard navigation link present.

- Page container and elements have correct IDs.
- Navigation link back to dashboard confirmed.

6. Edit Article (/edit_article)
- Edit article form with IDs: edit-article-form, article-title, article-content, btn-save-changes.

- Analytics data section present with performance metric elements: views-count, unique-visitors-count, average-read-time.

Defects and Issues:

- No obvious issues found in static templates, element IDs are consistent and appropriate.
- Some links use button onclick with window.location.href; could be improved to use anchor tags for accessibility.

Suggestions:

  [app.py] from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort from datetime import datetime  app = Flask(__name__)  # Mock data stores articles = {} article_versions = {} article_analytics_data = {}  # A simple auto-increment ID generator for articles and versions next_article_id = 1  # Article statuses STATUSES = ['draft', 'under_review', 'approved', 'rejected', 'published', 'archived']  # Categories example CATEGORIES = ['Technology', 'Science', 'Lifestyle', 'Health', 'Finance']   @app.route('/') def root():     # Redirect to dashboard     return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))   @app.route('/dashboard') def dashboard():     return render_template('dashboard.html')   @app.route('/create_article', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def create_article():     global next_article_id     if request.method == 'POST':         title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()         content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()         if not title or not content:             abort(400, 'Title and content are required')         article_id = next_article_id         next_article_id += 1         articles[article_id] = {             'id': article_id,             'title': title,             'content': content,             'status': 'draft',             'category': 'Uncategorized',             'last_modified': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),             'author': 'Current User',  # Placeholder             'published_date': None         }         # Initialize versions list         article_versions[article_id] = [             {                 'id': 1,                 'version_number': 1,                 'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),                 'stage': 'draft',                 'title': title,                 'content': content             }         ]         # Initialize analytics         article_analytics_data[article_id] = {             'views': 0,             'unique_visitors': 0,             'average_read_time': 0         }         return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))     else:         return render_template('create_article.html')   @app.route('/my_articles') def my_articles():     filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'all')     filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')      filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values()]     if filter_status != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]     if filter_category != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]      return render_template('my_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)   @app.route('/published_articles') def published_articles():     filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'published')     filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')      filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values() if a['status'] in ['published', 'archived']]     if filter_status != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]     if filter_category != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]      return render_template('published_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)   @app.route('/content_calendar') def content_calendar():     # For simplicity, we just render the page without dynamic data     return render_template('content_calendar.html')   @app.route('/edit_article/<int:article_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def edit_article(article_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')      if request.method == 'POST':         title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()         content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()         if not title or not content:             abort(400, 'Title and content are required')         article['title'] = title         article['content'] = content         article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')          # Save a new version         versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])         version_number = len(versions) + 1         new_version = {             'id': version_number,             'version_number': version_number,             'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),             'stage': article['status'],             'title': title,             'content': content         }         versions.append(new_version)         article_versions[article_id] = versions          return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))     else:         return render_template('edit_article.html', article=article)   @app.route('/version_history/<int:article_id>') def version_history(article_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')     versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])     return render_template('version_history.html', article=article, versions=versions)   @app.route('/restore_version/<int:article_id>/<int:version_id>', methods=['POST']) def restore_version(article_id, version_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')      versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])     version_to_restore = None     for v in versions:         if v['id'] == version_id:             version_to_restore = v             break      if not version_to_restore:         abort(404, 'Version not found')      # Restore content from version     article['title'] = version_to_restore['title']     article['content'] = version_to_restore['content']     article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')      # Save a new version as this restore event     version_number = len(versions) + 1     new_version = {         'id': version_number,         'version_number': version_number,         'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),         'stage': article['status'],         'title': article['title'],         'content': article['content']     }     versions.append(new_version)     article_versions[article_id] = versions      return redirect(url_for('edit_article', article_id=article_id))   @app.route('/article_analytics/<int:article_id>') def article_analytics(article_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')     analytics = article_analytics_data.get(article_id, {         'views': 0,         'unique_visitors': 0,         'average_read_time': 0     })     return render_template('article_analytics.html', article=article, analytics=analytics)   if __name__ == '__main__':     app.run(debug=True)

INPUT: === feedback_testing.txt ===
Functional Test Feedback for Content Publishing Hub

Due to the absence of backend source code (app.py), complete functional testing involving backend route execution, data processing, and dynamic content rendering cannot be performed. The following observations are based on thorough static inspection of template files starting from /dashboard and analysis of specified element IDs, navigation, and UI components.

1. Dashboard (/dashboard)
- All expected elements with correct IDs are present: dashboard-page, btn-create-article, btn-my-articles, btn-published-articles, btn-content-calendar, dashboard-overview.
- Navigation links to subpages exist and use proper ids.

2. Create Article (/create_article)
- The article creation form contains the proper input fields (article-title, article-content) and submit button (btn-submit-article) with correct method and action.
- Navigation button to return to dashboard exists and is correctly identified.

3. My Articles (/my_articles)
- Contains filter controls with the correct select elements for filtering by status and category.
- Displays articles in a table with well-defined columns and action buttons/links for editing, viewing versions, and analytics.
- Navigation elements to dashboard and create article exist.

4. Published Articles (/published_articles)
- Filter controls allow filtering by published and archived statuses with appropriate default selections.
- Articles table and navigation back to dashboard are present.

5. Content Calendar (/content_calendar)
- Calendar page displays a placeholder message and navigation link back to the dashboard.

6. Edit Article (/edit_article)
- Form for editing articles exists with input fields prefilled from backend placeholders.
- Has save changes button and back navigation to dashboard.

7. Version History (/version_history)
- Table lists article versions with columns including version number, date, stage, and actions.
- Each version row has a restore button.
- Navigation back to article editing page is present.

8. Article Analytics (/article_analytics)
- Displays analytics metrics including total views, unique visitors, and average read time.
- Navigation button back to article editing is present.

Defects and Limitations:
- Backend implementation source code (app.py) is missing, making it impossible to test backend functionality, form submission handling, database interactions, and actual data rendering.
- No automated or manual backend test execution can be performed.
- Button elements that perform navigation using onclick and window.location.href are not optimal for accessibility; anchor tags should be used instead.
- Accessibility features (ARIA roles, labels) are missing; forms and buttons could be improved for screen readers.
- No client-side validation scripts are present; relying only on HTML "required" attributes.
- Template dynamic values rely on backend context; without backend cannot validate data correctness or detect runtime errors.

Recommendations:
- Provide the Flask app.py source or API specification to enable end-to-end functional and integration testing.
- Implement automated functional tests for backend routes, database CRUD operations, and frontend interactions.
- Replace navigation buttons with anchor tags to improve accessibility.
- Add ARIA roles and client-side validation to enhance UI usability.
- Integrate backend analytics data binding and verify rendering and calculations.

Status: NEED_MODIFY


=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)

# Mock data stores
articles = {}
article_versions = {}
article_analytics_data = {}

# A simple auto-increment ID generator for articles and versions
next_article_id = 1

# Article statuses
STATUSES = ['draft', 'under_review', 'approved', 'rejected', 'published', 'archived']

# Categories example
CATEGORIES = ['Technology', 'Science', 'Lifestyle', 'Health', 'Finance']


@app.route('/')
def root():
    # Redirect to dashboard
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))


@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    return render_template('dashboard.html')


@app.route('/create_article', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def create_article():
    global next_article_id
    if request.method == 'POST':
        title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
        content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()
        if not title or not content:
            abort(400, 'Title and content are required')
        article_id = next_article_id
        next_article_id += 1
        articles[article_id] = {
            'id': article_id,
            'title': title,
            'content': content,
            'status': 'draft',
            'category': 'Uncategorized',
            'last_modified': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
            'author': 'Current User',  # Placeholder
            'published_date': None
        }
        # Initialize versions list
        article_versions[article_id] = [
            {
                'id': 1,
                'version_number': 1,
                'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
                'stage': 'draft',
                'title': title,
                'content': content
            }
        ]
        # Initialize analytics
        article_analytics_data[article_id] = {
            'views': 0,
            'unique_visitors': 0,
            'average_read_time': 0
        }
        return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))
    else:
        return render_template('create_article.html')


@app.route('/my_articles')
def my_articles():
    filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'all')
    filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')

    filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values()]
    if filter_status != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]
    if filter_category != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]

    return render_template('my_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)


@app.route('/published_articles')
def published_articles():
    filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'published')
    filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')

    filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values() if a['status'] in ['published', 'archived']]
    if filter_status != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]
    if filter_category != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]

    return render_template('published_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)


@app.route('/content_calendar')
def content_calendar():
    # For simplicity, we just render the page without dynamic data
    return render_template('content_calendar.html')


@app.route('/edit_article/<int:article_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def edit_article(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')

    if request.method == 'POST':
        title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
        content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()
        if not title or not content:
            abort(400, 'Title and content are required')
        article['title'] = title
        article['content'] = content
        article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

        # Save a new version
        versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
        version_number = len(versions) + 1
        new_version = {
            'id': version_number,
            'version_number': version_number,
            'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
            'stage': article['status'],
            'title': title,
            'content': content
        }
        versions.append(new_version)
        article_versions[article_id] = versions

        return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))
    else:
        return render_template('edit_article.html', article=article)


@app.route('/version_history/<int:article_id>')
def version_history(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')
    versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
    return render_template('version_history.html', article=article, versions=versions)


@app.route('/restore_version/<int:article_id>/<int:version_id>', methods=['POST'])
def restore_version(article_id, version_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')

    versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
    version_to_restore = None
    for v in versions:
        if v['id'] == version_id:
            version_to_restore = v
            break

    if not version_to_restore:
        abort(404, 'Version not found')

    # Restore content from version
    article['title'] = version_to_restore['title']
    article['content'] = version_to_restore['content']
    article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

    # Save a new version as this restore event
    version_number = len(versions) + 1
    new_version = {
        'id': version_number,
        'version_number': version_number,
        'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
        'stage': article['status'],
        'title': article['title'],
        'content': article['content']
    }
    versions.append(new_version)
    article_versions[article_id] = versions

    return redirect(url_for('edit_article', article_id=article_id))


@app.route('/article_analytics/<int:article_id>')
def article_analytics(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')
    analytics = article_analytics_data.get(article_id, {
        'views': 0,
        'unique_visitors': 0,
        'average_read_time': 0
    })
    return render_template('article_analytics.html', article=article, analytics=analytics)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)

  [app.py] from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort from datetime import datetime  app = Flask(__name__)  # Mock data stores articles = {} article_versions = {} article_analytics_data = {}  # A simple auto-increment ID generator for articles and versions next_article_id = 1  # Article statuses STATUSES = ['draft', 'under_review', 'approved', 'rejected', 'published', 'archived']  # Categories example CATEGORIES = ['Technology', 'Science', 'Lifestyle', 'Health', 'Finance']   @app.route('/') def root():     # Redirect to dashboard     return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))   @app.route('/dashboard') def dashboard():     return render_template('dashboard.html')   @app.route('/create_article', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def create_article():     global next_article_id     if request.method == 'POST':         title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()         content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()         if not title or not content:             abort(400, 'Title and content are required')         article_id = next_article_id         next_article_id += 1         articles[article_id] = {             'id': article_id,             'title': title,             'content': content,             'status': 'draft',             'category': 'Uncategorized',             'last_modified': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),             'author': 'Current User',  # Placeholder             'published_date': None         }         # Initialize versions list         article_versions[article_id] = [             {                 'id': 1,                 'version_number': 1,                 'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),                 'stage': 'draft',                 'title': title,                 'content': content             }         ]         # Initialize analytics         article_analytics_data[article_id] = {             'views': 0,             'unique_visitors': 0,             'average_read_time': 0         }         return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))     else:         return render_template('create_article.html')   @app.route('/my_articles') def my_articles():     filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'all')     filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')      filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values()]     if filter_status != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]     if filter_category != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]      return render_template('my_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)   @app.route('/published_articles') def published_articles():     filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'published')     filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')      filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values() if a['status'] in ['published', 'archived']]     if filter_status != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]     if filter_category != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]      return render_template('published_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)   @app.route('/content_calendar') def content_calendar():     # For simplicity, we just render the page without dynamic data     return render_template('content_calendar.html')   @app.route('/edit_article/<int:article_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def edit_article(article_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')      if request.method == 'POST':         title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()         content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()         if not title or not content:             abort(400, 'Title and content are required')         article['title'] = title         article['content'] = content         article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')          # Save a new version         versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])         version_number = len(versions) + 1         new_version = {             'id': version_number,             'version_number': version_number,             'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),             'stage': article['status'],             'title': title,             'content': content         }         versions.append(new_version)         article_versions[article_id] = versions          return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))     else:         return render_template('edit_article.html', article=article)   @app.route('/version_history/<int:article_id>') def version_history(article_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')     versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])     return render_template('version_history.html', article=article, versions=versions)   @app.route('/restore_version/<int:article_id>/<int:version_id>', methods=['POST']) def restore_version(article_id, version_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')      versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])     version_to_restore = None     for v in versions:         if v['id'] == version_id:             version_to_restore = v             break      if not version_to_restore:         abort(404, 'Version not found')      # Restore content from version     article['title'] = version_to_restore['title']     article['content'] = version_to_restore['content']     article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')      # Save a new version as this restore event     version_number = len(versions) + 1     new_version = {         'id': version_number,         'version_number': version_number,         'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),         'stage': article['status'],         'title': article['title'],         'content': article['content']     }     versions.append(new_version)     article_versions[article_id] = versions      return redirect(url_for('edit_article', article_id=article_id))   @app.route('/article_analytics/<int:article_id>') def article_analytics(article_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')     analytics = article_analytics_data.get(article_id, {         'views': 0,         'unique_visitors': 0,         'average_read_time': 0     })     return render_template('article_analytics.html', article=article, analytics=analytics)   if __name__ == '__main__':     app.run(debug=True)

Recommendations: - Provide the Flask app.py source or API specification to enable end-to-end functional and integration testing. - Implement automated functional tests for backend routes, database CRUD operations, and frontend interactions. - Replace navigation buttons with anchor tags to improve accessibility. - Add ARIA roles and client-side validation to enhance UI usability. - Integrate backend analytics data binding and verify rendering and calculations. from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)

# Mock data stores
articles = {}
article_versions = {}
article_analytics_data = {}

# A simple auto-increment ID generator for articles and versions
next_article_id = 1

# Article statuses
STATUSES = ['draft', 'under_review', 'approved', 'rejected', 'published', 'archived']

# Categories example
CATEGORIES = ['Technology', 'Science', 'Lifestyle', 'Health', 'Finance']


@app.route('/')
def root():
    # Redirect to dashboard
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))


@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    return render_template('dashboard.html')


@app.route('/create_article', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def create_article():
    global next_article_id
    if request.method == 'POST':
        title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
        content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()
        if not title or not content:
            abort(400, 'Title and content are required')
        article_id = next_article_id
        next_article_id += 1
        articles[article_id] = {
            'id': article_id,
            'title': title,
            'content': content,
            'status': 'draft',
            'category': 'Uncategorized',
            'last_modified': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
            'author': 'Current User',  # Placeholder
            'published_date': None
        }
        # Initialize versions list
        article_versions[article_id] = [
            {
                'id': 1,
                'version_number': 1,
                'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
                'stage': 'draft',
                'title': title,
                'content': content
            }
        ]
        # Initialize analytics
        article_analytics_data[article_id] = {
            'views': 0,
            'unique_visitors': 0,
            'average_read_time': 0
        }
        return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))
    else:
        return render_template('create_article.html')


@app.route('/my_articles')
def my_articles():
    filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'all')
    filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')

    filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values()]
    if filter_status != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]
    if filter_category != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]

    return render_template('my_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)


@app.route('/published_articles')
def published_articles():
    filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'published')
    filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')

    filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values() if a['status'] in ['published', 'archived']]
    if filter_status != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]
    if filter_category != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]

    return render_template('published_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)


@app.route('/content_calendar')
def content_calendar():
    # For simplicity, we just render the page without dynamic data
    return render_template('content_calendar.html')


@app.route('/edit_article/<int:article_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def edit_article(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')

    if request.method == 'POST':
        title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
        content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()
        if not title or not content:
            abort(400, 'Title and content are required')
        article['title'] = title
        article['content'] = content
        article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

        # Save a new version
        versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
        version_number = len(versions) + 1
        new_version = {
            'id': version_number,
            'version_number': version_number,
            'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
            'stage': article['status'],
            'title': title,
            'content': content
        }
        versions.append(new_version)
        article_versions[article_id] = versions

        return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))
    else:
        return render_template('edit_article.html', article=article)


@app.route('/version_history/<int:article_id>')
def version_history(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')
    versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
    return render_template('version_history.html', article=article, versions=versions)


@app.route('/restore_version/<int:article_id>/<int:version_id>', methods=['POST'])
def restore_version(article_id, version_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')

    versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
    version_to_restore = None
    for v in versions:
        if v['id'] == version_id:
            version_to_restore = v
            break

    if not version_to_restore:
        abort(404, 'Version not found')

    # Restore content from version
    article['title'] = version_to_restore['title']
    article['content'] = version_to_restore['content']
    article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

    # Save a new version as this restore event
    version_number = len(versions) + 1
    new_version = {
        'id': version_number,
        'version_number': version_number,
        'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
        'stage': article['status'],
        'title': article['title'],
        'content': article['content']
    }
    versions.append(new_version)
    article_versions[article_id] = versions

    return redirect(url_for('edit_article', article_id=article_id))


@app.route('/article_analytics/<int:article_id>')
def article_analytics(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')
    analytics = article_analytics_data.get(article_id, {
        'views': 0,
        'unique_visitors': 0,
        'average_read_time': 0
    })
    return render_template('article_analytics.html', article=article, analytics=analytics)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)

Functional Test Feedback for Content Publishing Hub

Due to the absence of backend source code (app.py), complete functional testing involving backend route execution, data processing, and dynamic content rendering cannot be performed. The following observations are based on thorough static inspection of template files starting from /dashboard and analysis of specified element IDs, navigation, and UI components.

1. Dashboard (/dashboard)
- All expected elements with correct IDs are present: dashboard-page, btn-create-article, btn-my-articles, btn-published-articles, btn-content-calendar, dashboard-overview.
- Navigation links to subpages exist and use proper ids.

2. Create Article (/create_article)
- The article creation form contains the proper input fields (article-title, article-content) and submit button (btn-submit-article) with correct method and action.
- Navigation button to return to dashboard exists and is correctly identified.

3. My Articles (/my_articles)
- Contains filter controls with the correct select elements for filtering by status and category.
- Displays articles in a table with well-defined columns and action buttons/links for editing, viewing versions, and analytics.
- Navigation elements to dashboard and create article exist.

4. Published Articles (/published_articles)
- Filter controls allow filtering by published and archived statuses with appropriate default selections.
- Articles table and navigation back to dashboard are present.

5. Content Calendar (/content_calendar)
- Calendar page displays a placeholder message and navigation link back to the dashboard.

6. Edit Article (/edit_article)
- Form for editing articles exists with input fields prefilled from backend placeholders.
- Has save changes button and back navigation to dashboard.

7. Version History (/version_history)
- Table lists article versions with columns including version number, date, stage, and actions.
- Each version row has a restore button.
- Navigation back to article editing page is present.

8. Article Analytics (/article_analytics)
- Displays analytics metrics including total views, unique visitors, and average read time.
- Navigation button back to article editing is present.

Defects and Limitations:
- Backend implementation source code (app.py) is missing, making it impossible to test backend functionality, form submission handling, database interactions, and actual data rendering.
- No automated or manual backend test execution can be performed.
- Button elements that perform navigation using onclick and window.location.href are not optimal for accessibility; anchor tags should be used instead.
- Accessibility features (ARIA roles, labels) are missing; forms and buttons could be improved for screen readers.
- No client-side validation scripts are present; relying only on HTML "required" attributes.
- Template dynamic values rely on backend context; without backend cannot validate data correctness or detect runtime errors.

Recommendations:
- Provide the Flask app.py source or API specification to enable end-to-end functional and integration testing.
- Implement automated functional tests for backend routes, database CRUD operations, and frontend interactions.
- Replace navigation buttons with anchor tags to improve accessibility.
- Add ARIA roles and client-side validation to enhance UI usability.
- Integrate backend analytics data binding and verify rendering and calculations.

  [app.py] from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort from datetime import datetime  app = Flask(__name__)  # Mock data stores articles = {} article_versions = {} article_analytics_data = {}  # A simple auto-increment ID generator for articles and versions next_article_id = 1  # Article statuses STATUSES = ['draft', 'under_review', 'approved', 'rejected', 'published', 'archived']  # Categories example CATEGORIES = ['Technology', 'Science', 'Lifestyle', 'Health', 'Finance']   @app.route('/') def root():     # Redirect to dashboard     return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))   @app.route('/dashboard') def dashboard():     return render_template('dashboard.html')   @app.route('/create_article', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def create_article():     global next_article_id     if request.method == 'POST':         title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()         content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()         if not title or not content:             abort(400, 'Title and content are required')         article_id = next_article_id         next_article_id += 1         articles[article_id] = {             'id': article_id,             'title': title,             'content': content,             'status': 'draft',             'category': 'Uncategorized',             'last_modified': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),             'author': 'Current User',  # Placeholder             'published_date': None         }         # Initialize versions list         article_versions[article_id] = [             {                 'id': 1,                 'version_number': 1,                 'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),                 'stage': 'draft',                 'title': title,                 'content': content             }         ]         # Initialize analytics         article_analytics_data[article_id] = {             'views': 0,             'unique_visitors': 0,             'average_read_time': 0         }         return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))     else:         return render_template('create_article.html')   @app.route('/my_articles') def my_articles():     filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'all')     filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')      filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values()]     if filter_status != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]     if filter_category != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]      return render_template('my_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)   @app.route('/published_articles') def published_articles():     filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'published')     filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')      filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values() if a['status'] in ['published', 'archived']]     if filter_status != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]     if filter_category != 'all':         filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]      return render_template('published_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)   @app.route('/content_calendar') def content_calendar():     # For simplicity, we just render the page without dynamic data     return render_template('content_calendar.html')   @app.route('/edit_article/<int:article_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def edit_article(article_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')      if request.method == 'POST':         title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()         content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()         if not title or not content:             abort(400, 'Title and content are required')         article['title'] = title         article['content'] = content         article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')          # Save a new version         versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])         version_number = len(versions) + 1         new_version = {             'id': version_number,             'version_number': version_number,             'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),             'stage': article['status'],             'title': title,             'content': content         }         versions.append(new_version)         article_versions[article_id] = versions          return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))     else:         return render_template('edit_article.html', article=article)   @app.route('/version_history/<int:article_id>') def version_history(article_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')     versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])     return render_template('version_history.html', article=article, versions=versions)   @app.route('/restore_version/<int:article_id>/<int:version_id>', methods=['POST']) def restore_version(article_id, version_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')      versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])     version_to_restore = None     for v in versions:         if v['id'] == version_id:             version_to_restore = v             break      if not version_to_restore:         abort(404, 'Version not found')      # Restore content from version     article['title'] = version_to_restore['title']     article['content'] = version_to_restore['content']     article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')      # Save a new version as this restore event     version_number = len(versions) + 1     new_version = {         'id': version_number,         'version_number': version_number,         'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),         'stage': article['status'],         'title': article['title'],         'content': article['content']     }     versions.append(new_version)     article_versions[article_id] = versions      return redirect(url_for('edit_article', article_id=article_id))   @app.route('/article_analytics/<int:article_id>') def article_analytics(article_id):     article = articles.get(article_id)     if not article:         abort(404, 'Article not found')     analytics = article_analytics_data.get(article_id, {         'views': 0,         'unique_visitors': 0,         'average_read_time': 0     })     return render_template('article_analytics.html', article=article, analytics=analytics)   if __name__ == '__main__':     app.run(debug=True)

INPUT: === feedback_testing.txt ===
Functional Test Feedback for Content Publishing Hub

Starting from /dashboard, comprehensive testing of the provided templates was performed by static verification of element presence, IDs, navigation links, and UI components. However, dynamic backend testing including route execution, data processing, persistence, and form handling could not be performed due to absence of the backend source code (app.py).

1. Dashboard Page (/dashboard):
- IDs dashboard-page, btn-create-article, btn-my-articles, btn-published-articles, btn-content-calendar, dashboard-overview are present.
- Navigation links direct to appropriate pages via URL generation placeholders.

2. Create Article Page (/create_article):
- Contains form with method POST and action URL placeholder.
- Input fields for title and content correctly have IDs article-title and article-content.
- Submit button with ID btn-submit-article is present.
- Navigation back to dashboard uses button with onclick attributing window.location.href.

3. My Articles Page (/my_articles):
- Filtering controls present with IDs filter-status, filter-category, and btn-apply-filters.
- Articles table with ID my-articles-table has columns (Title, Status, Category, Last Modified, Actions).
- Action links for version history and analytics have correct IDs referencing article IDs.
- Navigation buttons to dashboard and create article are present with expected IDs.

4. Published Articles Page (/published_articles):
- Filtering form present with controls to filter status and category.
- Published articles table with proper headings and rows using valid IDs.
- Navigation back to dashboard button presents.

5. Content Calendar Page (/content_calendar):
- Page includes ID content-calendar-page.
- Navigation back to dashboard link is present.
- Placeholder text for calendar schedule is shown.

6. Edit Article Page (/edit_article):
- Edit form with pre-populated article title and content fields.
- IDs are consistent and correct for form and input elements.
- Save changes button and back to dashboard button present.

7. Version History Page (/version_history):
- Versions table lists versions with columns: Version Number, Date, Stage, Actions.
- Restore buttons exist with distinct IDs per version.
- Navigation back to editing page is provided.

8. Article Analytics Page (/article_analytics):
- Page shows analytics metrics with element IDs views-count, unique-visitors-count, average-read-time.
- Back to article editing button present.

Defects and Observations:
- Backend routes, logic, and database interactions cannot be validated or tested due to missing app.py file.
- Form submission, filtering, version restore, and analytics data rendering functionalities remain untested.
- Usage of button elements with onclick navigation is not ideal for accessibility; anchor tags should replace these.
- No accessibility ARIA attributes or semantic roles defined in templates.
- No client-side input validation or error messaging scripts are included.

Suggestions:
- Provide backend source code or API endpoints to enable functional integration testing.
- Replace navigational buttons using onclick with semantic anchor links.
- Add ARIA roles and accessibility enhancements.
- Implement client-side validation for form inputs.
- Develop automated tests for backend route correctness, data consistency, and workflow correctness.

Status: NEED_MODIFY


=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)

# Mock data stores
articles = {}
article_versions = {}
article_analytics_data = {}

# A simple auto-increment ID generator for articles and versions
next_article_id = 1

# Article statuses
STATUSES = ['draft', 'under_review', 'approved', 'rejected', 'published', 'archived']

# Categories example
CATEGORIES = ['Technology', 'Science', 'Lifestyle', 'Health', 'Finance']


@app.route('/')
def root():
    # Redirect to dashboard
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))


@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    return render_template('dashboard.html')


@app.route('/create_article', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def create_article():
    global next_article_id
    if request.method == 'POST':
        title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
        content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()
        if not title or not content:
            abort(400, 'Title and content are required')
        article_id = next_article_id
        next_article_id += 1
        articles[article_id] = {
            'id': article_id,
            'title': title,
            'content': content,
            'status': 'draft',
            'category': 'Uncategorized',
            'last_modified': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
            'author': 'Current User',  # Placeholder
            'published_date': None
        }
        # Initialize versions list
        article_versions[article_id] = [
            {
                'id': 1,
                'version_number': 1,
                'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
                'stage': 'draft',
                'title': title,
                'content': content
            }
        ]
        # Initialize analytics
        article_analytics_data[article_id] = {
            'views': 0,
            'unique_visitors': 0,
            'average_read_time': 0
        }
        return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))
    else:
        return render_template('create_article.html')


@app.route('/my_articles')
def my_articles():
    filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'all')
    filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')

    filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values()]
    if filter_status != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]
    if filter_category != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]

    return render_template('my_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)


@app.route('/published_articles')
def published_articles():
    filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'published')
    filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')

    filtered_articles = [a for a in articles.values() if a['status'] in ['published', 'archived']]
    if filter_status != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['status'] == filter_status]
    if filter_category != 'all':
        filtered_articles = [a for a in filtered_articles if a['category'] == filter_category]

    return render_template('published_articles.html', articles=filtered_articles, categories=CATEGORIES)


@app.route('/content_calendar')
def content_calendar():
    # For simplicity, we just render the page without dynamic data
    return render_template('content_calendar.html')


@app.route('/edit_article/<int:article_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def edit_article(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')

    if request.method == 'POST':
        title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
        content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()
        if not title or not content:
            abort(400, 'Title and content are required')
        article['title'] = title
        article['content'] = content
        article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

        # Save a new version
        versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
        version_number = len(versions) + 1
        new_version = {
            'id': version_number,
            'version_number': version_number,
            'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
            'stage': article['status'],
            'title': title,
            'content': content
        }
        versions.append(new_version)
        article_versions[article_id] = versions

        return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))
    else:
        return render_template('edit_article.html', article=article)


@app.route('/version_history/<int:article_id>')
def version_history(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')
    versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
    return render_template('version_history.html', article=article, versions=versions)


@app.route('/restore_version/<int:article_id>/<int:version_id>', methods=['POST'])
def restore_version(article_id, version_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')

    versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
    version_to_restore = None
    for v in versions:
        if v['id'] == version_id:
            version_to_restore = v
            break

    if not version_to_restore:
        abort(404, 'Version not found')

    # Restore content from version
    article['title'] = version_to_restore['title']
    article['content'] = version_to_restore['content']
    article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

    # Save a new version as this restore event
    version_number = len(versions) + 1
    new_version = {
        'id': version_number,
        'version_number': version_number,
        'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
        'stage': article['status'],
        'title': article['title'],
        'content': article['content']
    }
    versions.append(new_version)
    article_versions[article_id] = versions

    return redirect(url_for('edit_article', article_id=article_id))


@app.route('/article_analytics/<int:article_id>')
def article_analytics(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404, 'Article not found')
    analytics = article_analytics_data.get(article_id, {
        'views': 0,
        'unique_visitors': 0,
        'average_read_time': 0
    })
    return render_template('article_analytics.html', article=article, analytics=analytics)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)

INPUT: === app.py ===
from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, abort
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)

# Data structures to simulate database
articles = {}
article_versions = {}
article_analytics_data = {}

# Auto-increment IDs
next_article_id = 1

# Predefined statuses and categories
STATUSES = ['draft', 'under_review', 'approved', 'rejected', 'published', 'archived']
CATEGORIES = ['Technology', 'Science', 'Lifestyle', 'Health', 'Finance', 'Uncategorized']

@app.route('/')
def root():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))

@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    return render_template('dashboard.html')

@app.route('/create_article', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def create_article():
    global next_article_id
    if request.method == 'POST':
        title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
        content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()
        if not title or not content:
            abort(400, "Title and content are required.")
        article_id = next_article_id
        next_article_id += 1
        articles[article_id] = {
            'id': article_id,
            'title': title,
            'content': content,
            'status': 'draft',
            'category': 'Uncategorized',
            'last_modified': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
            'author': 'Current User',
            'published_date': None
        }
        article_versions[article_id] = [{
            'id': 1,
            'version_number': 1,
            'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
            'stage': 'draft',
            'title': title,
            'content': content
        }]
        article_analytics_data[article_id] = {
            'views': 0,
            'unique_visitors': 0,
            'average_read_time': 0
        }
        return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))

    return render_template('create_article.html')

@app.route('/my_articles')
def my_articles():
    filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'all')
    filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')

    filtered = list(articles.values())
    if filter_status != 'all':
        filtered = [a for a in filtered if a['status'] == filter_status]
    if filter_category != 'all':
        filtered = [a for a in filtered if a['category'] == filter_category]

    return render_template('my_articles.html', articles=filtered, categories=CATEGORIES)

@app.route('/published_articles')
def published_articles():
    filter_status = request.args.get('filter_status', 'published')
    filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', 'all')

    filtered = [a for a in articles.values() if a['status'] in ['published', 'archived']]
    if filter_status != 'all':
        filtered = [a for a in filtered if a['status'] == filter_status]
    if filter_category != 'all':
        filtered = [a for a in filtered if a['category'] == filter_category]

    return render_template('published_articles.html', articles=filtered, categories=CATEGORIES)

@app.route('/content_calendar')
def content_calendar():
    return render_template('content_calendar.html')

@app.route('/edit_article/<int:article_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def edit_article(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404)

    if request.method == 'POST':
        title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
        content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()
        if not title or not content:
            abort(400, "Title and content are required.")
        article['title'] = title
        article['content'] = content
        article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

        versions = article_versions.setdefault(article_id, [])
        version_num = len(versions) + 1
        versions.append({
            'id': version_num,
            'version_number': version_num,
            'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
            'stage': article['status'],
            'title': title,
            'content': content
        })
        article_versions[article_id] = versions

        return redirect(url_for('my_articles'))

    return render_template('edit_article.html', article=article)

@app.route('/version_history/<int:article_id>')
def version_history(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404)
    versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
    return render_template('version_history.html', article=article, versions=versions)

@app.route('/restore_version/<int:article_id>/<int:version_id>', methods=['POST'])
def restore_version(article_id, version_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404)
    versions = article_versions.get(article_id, [])
    version_to_restore = None
    for v in versions:
        if v['id'] == version_id:
            version_to_restore = v
            break
    if not version_to_restore:
        abort(404)

    article['title'] = version_to_restore['title']
    article['content'] = version_to_restore['content']
    article['last_modified'] = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

    version_num = len(versions) + 1
    versions.append({
        'id': version_num,
        'version_number': version_num,
        'date': datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
        'stage': article['status'],
        'title': article['title'],
        'content': article['content']
    })
    article_versions[article_id] = versions

    return redirect(url_for('edit_article', article_id=article_id))

@app.route('/article_analytics/<int:article_id>')
def article_analytics(article_id):
    article = articles.get(article_id)
    if not article:
        abort(404)

    analytics = article_analytics_data.get(article_id, {
        'views': 0,
        'unique_visitors': 0,
        'average_read_time': 0
    })

    return render_template('article_analytics.html', article=article, analytics=analytics)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
